Moreover, your granddaughter’s virtue follows the legacy of her forebears, delighting in the zither’s charm like Bian of old. My grandson, raised on poetry and books, has yet to wield his brush to compose. Though this is a matter of kinship, why should age be a barrier? She may serve as Huang’s matchmaker, and all will call her the true wife of Liang.

Speak of love only when the time is right, offering fern and artemisia in dutiful service. As rites value simplicity, I humbly prepare hazelnuts and chestnuts to announce the betrothal. My modest gifts are listed on the right—with respect, I present this proposal for your consideration. May your esteemed kindness deign to reflect upon it.

**Raising the Ridgepole Address**
As the Three Mountains converge, all proclaim this blessed land of great peace. From a single vein of lineage, the Dao’s gate follows the hidden path. Now, entrusted with the duty of the ancestral hall, we complete the work of building a home. The oracle and tortoise shell align with the auspicious hexagram; the people’s fondness for magpies and crows manifests as omens upon the roof.

With reverence, I consider [Name], who carries on the family legacy, his name sung in praise. In his hand, the jade tablet emerges from the brush’s artistry; in his heart, he holds the framework’s grand design. From a single household’s affairs, we rejoice in the splendor of the twin-petal tower. Sheltered within a hundred *li*, we celebrate the glory of the flowery county.

One day’s renewal brings ten thousand years of magnificence. As a humble craftsman, I dare not claim great wisdom. Following the given path, I plan and construct—how could I presume to saw or hew at will? In the marketplace of gold, they vie to boast of Fan Li’s wealth. Before the hall of colorful robes, I wish to emulate Lao Lai’s play.

Let me offer the sparrow’s modest congratulations for the new hall, and ascend the rainbow’s high ridgepole. As the poem says:
*Like you, the timber is fit for ridgepole and beam—*
*Yet it still requires skillful carving.*
*A great mansion shelters ten thousand, vast in its refuge,*
*And in the courtyard, we rejoice in the triple sophora’s shade.*

**End of Xu Xian’s Literary Anthology, Scroll Thirteen**
**Xu Xian’s Literary Anthology, Scroll Fourteen**

**Lamp Couplets for the Ridgepole**

**Ridgepole Couplets**
For this palace:
May the sagely lord’s myriad-year Dao forever bring peace to the Central Lands,
May the luminous spirits’ singular virtue bestow blessings upon the state and household.

The phoenix’s fortune stretches long, eternally inscribing ten thousand years of prosperity,
The turtle-mountain’s grandeur stands firm, safeguarding the four borders in everlasting peace.

Renewing the old to restore the grand design,
When adversity reaches its peak, fortune returns—kindred aspirations are fulfilled.

**Hall of Fixed Light**
The Buddha’s compassion pervades the three thousand great thousand worlds,
Divine power, vast and boundless, protects the temple halls for ten thousand ages.

**Temple of the Rain-Praying King**
May the sagely Son of Heaven’s life endure as long as heaven and earth, his sacred longevity boundless,
May the Rain-Praying King bring timely rains and gentle winds—his divine spirit ever responsive.

**Celebratory Lamp Couplets**
May the emperor’s reign span ten thousand years, as enduring as the seas and mountains,
May the realm’s eight directions be open and connected, its carts and books sharing the same Dao.

May the sagely lord’s longevity be ever secure, the Southern Dipper’s star presenting auspicious signs,
May the divine radiance appear thrice, the Eastern Marchmount’s eight characters shining brighter.

When the august one establishes the ultimate standard, heaven and earth follow the four seasons’ order,
When great virtue is called "life," the people are nurtured and the five grains ripen.

The sage possesses great virtue—longevity, wealth, and many sons,
The world becomes one family, its borders well-governed, its seas united.

The imperial capital’s splendor coils like a dragon, crouches like a tiger, its might weighing ten thousand jun,
The realm enjoys great peace—barking dogs and crowing roosters resound across the four seas.

Our dynasty unifies all from north to south, heaven vast and earth broad,
The world knows peace once more, customs refined and winds pure as in ancient times.

A flourishing era of civil brilliance—this is the time of great peace,
Bountiful harvests of fine grain bring joy to the eastern farmers in this year of plenty.

**Golden Palace’s Birthday Celebration**
The Golden Palace’s transformation body manifests eighty-two forms, all sharing the same name and title,
A jade goblet offers longevity—sixteen thousand years become spring and autumn.

Penglai is entirely home to immortals, their names inscribed on the cinnabar terrace,
The Southern Dipper’s Old Man Star appears, its light joining the Eastern Well.

**Jade Palace’s Birthday Celebration**
On the great celebration of the seventh month’s Zhongyuan,
Five winds and ten rains mark a time of peace, jade candles present auspicious signs.

Heaven-born ministers yield to Lord Lai, granting him a day’s precedence,
Thunderous cheers echo Zhuangzi’s eight-thousand-autumn blessing.

Five-colored auspicious clouds appear in splendid omens,
Triple harvests bring joy in celebrating great peace.

The Jade Palace’s clouds part, heaven lies close at hand,
The Silver River’s waters bathe the moon in clear radiance.

Heaven’s seal is written in cinnabar phoenix script,
Earth’s grandeur rises in the towering turtle-mountain.

**Hall of Harmonious Kinship**
Baskets and stands preserve the Zhou rites,
Robes and caps restore the Han’s majestic bearing.

Lofty integrity and perfect reputation shine like the sun,
A hall filled with harmonious qi is a single sphere of spring.

Literature is an eternal endeavor,
Loyalty and filial piety are a lifetime’s devotion.

Reputation endures like the sun and moon,
Dao and righteousness weigh as heavily as mountains.

The divine tree remains evergreen,
The cinnamon tree delights in passing on its fragrance.

**Hall of Childbirth**
Immortal consorts gather at the Jasper Pool feast,
Men must study the jade-slab classics.

The thousand-year peach of the Dark Garden presents auspicious signs,
The ten-thousand-year cassia of Yan Mountain transmits its fragrance.

Mulberry and catalpa share the shade of the village shrine,
Orchids and irises flourish abundantly in the courtyard.

The family legacy is passed down through generations,
A single arrow strengthens the resolve of sons.

**Celebrating the Lantern Festival Couplets**
Heaven unfolds the phoenix calendar—may the nation and altars endure for ten thousand years,
Earth embraces the turtle-mountain—lanterns and towers illuminate the fifteenth night.

On the Lantern Festival’s radiant evening, carriages and horses bring three thousand guests,
The turtle-mountain’s resplendent decorations crown the southeast’s foremost peak.

Ten thousand bushels of lotus lanterns—towers and the night moon’s shadows intertwine,
Three coins for a peck of rice—village shrines and spring winds bring joy to the people.

Penglai’s three isles, where immortals dwell—palaces here are noble,
The Eastern Wall’s two stars, repository of texts—the Milky Way’s literary splendor.

The ancestral temple’s solemn rites have been observed for four hundred years,
The first month’s harmony begins on the fifteenth night—the Lantern Festival’s feast and revelry.

The sun’s brilliance adorns banners with golden characters,
Clouds part at the heavenly gates, revealing the jade brush’s radiance.

Temple sacrifices preserve ancient rites for a thousand years,
Proclamations of honor are inscribed in lavish gold script.

**Lamp Couplets**
The Perfected Lord receives the register—may the emperor’s longevity match heaven and earth’s endurance,
The Heavenly Master’s Dao is revered—may the sun and moon shine brightly for a hundred generations.

The sagely lord ushers in great peace—may his life rival the Southern Mountains, his blessings flow like the Eastern Sea,
The immortal Dao remains ever auspicious—his name inscribed on the cinnabar terrace, his body dwelling in the Red City.

The jasper palaces’ twin towers stand a foot from heaven, ascending the cloud ladder with ease,
A golden missive arrives from the sun’s edge, its radiance outshining the stars.

Purified through fasting and bathing, serve the Supreme Emperor with an undivided heart,
"Intelligent, bright, upright, and correct"—such is the spirit that receives its due virtue.

The purple clay proclaims the imperial decree, displaying the divine radiance of new honors,
Blue cloth forms the net of talismans—ancient prophecies and figures in lavish splendor.

**Universal Salvation Ritual**
May the present emperor’s reign endure for ten thousand years, his power as stable as bedrock,
May the Primordial Heavenly Worthy expound the scriptures ten times, his light manifesting in precious pearls.

Mount Tai stands majestic, the four peaks’ revered site—fasting for a single day,
The Great Canopy stretches boundless above the three realms—universally delivering all beings.

The divine capital spans eighteen thousand miles, the four lands coming to pay homage,
The seventy-two bureaus of Mount Tai deliver all beings.

A single yellow cloud congeals in the spirit’s abode,
Three thousand measures of sweet dew universally open the gates of salvation.

May the sagely lord’s life equal heaven’s, the cosmos enduring for ten thousand generations,
May Laozi take the Dao as his foundation, the four directions’ sun and moon ever bright.

**Couplets for the Lonely Spirits’ Lamps**
The Eastern Wondrous Severity Palace manifests transformations across the ten directions, light revealing auspicious signs,
The Western Na Kingdom’s Maitreya and Great Brahma vow to deliver all beings.

Purified through fasting and bathing, serve the Supreme Emperor with an undivided heart,
The departed souls ascend directly to the Southern Palace, attaining the wondrous Dao.

On the Jade Capital Mountain, heaven lies but a foot and a half away, piercing straight through the Dark Capital,
The Ganges’ sands span the earth—all worlds together ride the wondrous Dao.

The Great Canopy stretches boundless above the three realms, the nine qi swirling and dense,
Mount Tai stands majestic, the four peaks’ revered site—ten thousand spirits come to pay homage.

A single pearl the size of a millet grain—ten directions’ worlds together behold its light,
Several cases of jade scriptures—hundreds of ancestors and ten thousand generations all receive deliverance.

The Eastern Florescence’s pure realm, the Western Na Kingdom—upholding precepts and practicing fasting,
The Southern Prosperity’s high office, the Northern Capital’s Cold Pool—saving the living and delivering the dead.

A single libation of cool, sweet dew,
Ninefold mysteries ascend the Upper Clarity’s thoroughfare.

Eight colors and nine chapters reveal the wondrous Dao,
Hundreds of ancestors and ten thousand generations ascend the Vermilion Palace.

The three paths of suffering are liberated, transcending the three realms,
Eight-colored radiance illuminates the eight directions.

Hearing the scriptures and listening to the Dharma, together we arouse compassion,
Sharing food and clothing, all equally enjoy warmth and sustenance.

The Blood Bowl Assembly—Mulian repays his mother’s kindness, his filial piety reaching through heaven and earth, his divine powers unmatched;
Earth Treasury presides as Teaching Master, his Dharma pervading the worlds as numerous as the sands of the Ganges, the Three Thousands.

*Xu Xian’s Literary Gems, Scroll Fourteen concludes*
